    <script type="text/ng-template" id="resource-status.html">
        <div ng-if="resource.accessPermitted && resource.noProgress">-</div>
        <div ng-if="resource.accessPermitted && !resource.noProgress">
            <!-- Documento 4-->
            <div ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'DocumentResource' && resource.accessPermitted">
                <span ng-if="resource.downloaded">
                    {{ 'Visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
                <span ng-if="!resource.downloaded">
                    {{ 'Não visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
                <!-- <span class="flex" ng-if="resource.downloaded">
                    <div class="prog">
                        <div class="progress-container lector-bg-lgray">
                            <div style="width:100%" class="progress-bar"></div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <span class="ml-10">100%</span>
                </span> -->
            </div>
            <!-- Gravação -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'EventResource' && resource.event['@class'] == 'RecordedEvent'">
                <div ng-if="resource.accessPermitted">
                    <span ng-if="resource.progress != null">{{ 'Visualizado' | translate }}	{{ resource.progress | number:2 }}%</span>
                    <span ng-if="resource.progress == null">{{ 'Não visualizado' | translate }}</span>
                </div>
            </span>
            <!-- Avaliação -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'EvaluationResource'">
                <span ng-if="isAttemptedEvaluation(resource) && resource.accessPermitted">
                    <span ng-if="isEvaluationPendingManualCheck(resource)">{{ 'Não corrigido' | translate }}</span>
                    <span ng-if="!isEvaluationPendingManualCheck(resource) && resource.approved">{{ 'Aprovado' | translate }} </span>
                    <span ng-if="!isEvaluationPendingManualCheck(resource) && !resource.approved">{{ 'Reprovado' | translate }} </span>
                </span>
                <span ng-if="!isAttemptedEvaluation(resource)">{{ 'Não realizado' | translate }}</span>
            </span>
            <!-- Avaliação de Reação -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'ReactionEvaluationResource'">
                <span ng-if="resource.answered">{{ 'Respondido' | translate }}</span>
                <span ng-if="!resource.answered">{{ 'Não respondido' | translate }}</span>
            </span>
            <!-- Webconferência -->
            <span ng-if="(resource['@class'] == 'EventResource' && resource.event['@class'] == 'LiveEvent') || 
                        resource['@class'] == 'LiveEventResource' && resource.accessPermitted">
                <div ng-if="resource.accessPermitted">
                    <span ng-if="resource.progress != null">{{ 'Acessado' | translate }} {{ resource.progress | number:2 }}%</span>
                    <span ng-if="resource.progress == null">{{ 'Não acessado' | translate }}</span>
                </div>
            </span>

            <div ng-if="((resource['@class'] == 'EvaluationResource' && !resource.maxed) || resource['@class'] == 'ReactionEvaluationResource') && resource.maxAttempts != null && evaluationsAttemptsTable != null">
                {{ 'Tentativas' | translate }}: {{ getEvaluationAttemptsLabel(resource) }}
            </div>

            <!-- Shareable Content Object -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'SCOResource'">
                <span ng-if="resource.status == 'COMPLETED'">{{ 'Completo' | translate }} </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.status == 'PASSED'">{{ 'Aprovado' | translate }} </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.status == 'INCOMPLETE'">{{ 'Incompleto' | translate }} </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.status == 'FAILED'">{{ 'Reprovado' | translate }} </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.status == 'BROWSED'">{{ 'Visualizado' | translate }} </span>
                <span ng-if="!resource.status || resource.status == 'NOT_ATTEMPTED'">{{ 'Não visualizado' | translate }} </span>
            </span>
            <!-- Vídeo - Link -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'VideoLinkResource'">
                <span ng-if="resource.progress">
                    {{ 'Visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
                <span ng-if="!resource.progress">
                    {{ 'Não visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
            </span>
            <!-- LTI -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'LtiResource'">
                <span ng-if="resource.progress == 100">
                    {{ 'Visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.progress != 100">
                    {{ 'Não visualizado' | translate }}
                </span>
            </span>

            <!-- Wiki -->
            <span ng-if="resource['@class'] == 'WikiResource'">
                <span ng-if="resource.progress == 100">
                    {{ 'Contribuído' | translate }}
                </span>
                <span ng-if="resource.progress != 100">
                    {{ 'Sem contribuição' | translate }}
                </span>
            </span>
        </div>
        <div class="lector-txt-accent" ng-if="!resource.accessPermitted">
            {{ 'Conteúdo obrigatório pendente' | translate }}
        </div>
